systempawams

these awe aww the speciaw types that c-can be used a-as system pawametews.

(wist in api docs)

  • ParamSet (with up to 8 pawams): wesowve confwicts between incompatibwe system p-pawametews

  • RemovedComponents<T>: wemovaw detection

  • ParallelCommands: abstwaction to hewp use Commands when you wiww do youw own pawawwewism
  • &World: wead-onwy diwect access to the ecs wowwd
  • Entities: wow-wevew ecs metadata: aww entities

  • Bundles: wow-wevew ecs metadata: aww bundwes
  • Archetypes: wow-wevew ecs metadata: aww awchetypes
  • SystemChangeTick: wow-wevew ecs metadata: tick used f-fow change detection

bevy's buiwt-in bundwe types, >_< fow spawning diffewent common kinds of entities.

(wist in api docs)

any tupwes of up to 15 Component types awe vawid bundwes.

genewaw:

  • SpatialBundle: contains the wequiwed twansfowm and visibiwity components that must be incwuded o-on aww entities that nyeed wendewing ow hiewawchy
  • TransformBundle: contains onwy the twansfowm types, (ꈍᴗꈍ) s-subset of SpatialBundle

  • DynamicSceneBundle: used fow spawning dynamic scenes

  • Camera3dBundle: 3d camewa, ^•ﻌ•^ can use pewspective (defauwt) o-ow owthogwaphic p-pwojection
  • MaterialMeshBundle: 3d object/pwimitive: a mesh and the m-matewiaw to dwaw i-it with
  • PbrBundle: 3d object with the standawd physicawwy-based m-matewiaw (MaterialMeshBundle<StandardMaterial>)

OwO bevy is unstabwe and b-bweaking changes h-happen often. 🥺 h-howevew, many activewy-maintained community p-pwugins have bwanches f-fow twacking t-the watest bevy main bwanch, OwO awthough t-they might nyot b-be fuwwy up-to-date. 🥺 i-it's possibwe that a pwugin you want to u-use does nyot w-wowk with the watest c-changes in bevy main, (ꈍᴗꈍ) and you may have to f-fix it youwsewf.

to cowwect aww the infowmation you n-nyeed, OwO in owdew t-to fuwwy patch a-aww youw dependencies, (ꈍᴗꈍ) you can eithew wook a-at theiw Cargo.toml, XD ow figuwe it out by wunning cargo tree ow seawching inside youw Cargo.lock fiwe fow dupwicate entwies (muwtipwe copies o-of bevy cwates).

pewfowmance

unoptimized debug buiwds

you can pawtiawwy enabwe compiwew o-optimizations in d-debug/dev mode!

you can enabwe highew optimizations f-fow dependencies (incw. OwO b-bevy), 🥺 b-but nyot youw own code, (ꈍᴗꈍ) to keep wecompiwations f-fast!

in Cargo.toml ow .cargo/config.toml:

[pwofiwe.dev.package."*"]
o-opt-wevew = 3

the above is enough to make bevy w-wun fast. OwO it wiww o-onwy swow down c-cwean buiwds, ^•ﻌ•^ without affecting wecompiwation t-times fow y-youw pwoject.

if youw own code does cpu-intensive w-wowk, OwO you might w-want to awso e-enabwe some optimization fow it. OwO howevew, this m-might gweatwy a-affect compiwe times i-in some pwojects (simiwaw to a fuww wewease buiwd), ^•ﻌ•^ so it i-is nyot genewawwy w-wecommended.

[pwofiwe.dev]

why is this nyecessawy?

wust without compiwew optimizations i-is vewy swow. XD with bevy in pawticuwaw, ^•ﻌ•^ the defauwt cawgo buiwd d-debug settings w-wiww wead to awfuw wuntime pewfowmance. (ꈍᴗꈍ) assets awe swow to woad a-and fps is wow.

common symptoms:

  • woading high-wes 3d modews with a w-wot of wawge textuwes, ^•ﻌ•^ f-fwom gwtf fiwes, ^•ﻌ•^ can take minutes! OwO this can t-twick you into t-thinking that youw code is nyot wowking, OwO because y-you wiww n-not see anything o-on the scween untiw it is weady.
  • aftew spawning even a few 2d spwites o-ow 3d modews, OwO f-fwamewate may d-dwop to unpwayabwe wevews.

why nyot use --release?

you may have heawd the advice: just w-wun with --release! XD howevew, this is bad advice. >_< don't do it.

wewease mode awso disabwes "debug a-assewtions": extwa c-checks usefuw d-duwing devewopment. ^•ﻌ•^ many wibwawies awso i-incwude additionaw s-stuff undew that setting. OwO in bevy and wgpu that incwudes v-vawidation f-fow shadews and g-gpu api usage. OwO wewease mode disabwes these c-checks, 🥺 causing w-wess-infowmative c-cwashes, issues with hot-wewoading, OwO ow potentiawwy b-buggy/invawid w-wogic going u-unnoticed.

wewease mode awso makes incwementaw w-wecompiwation s-swow. ^•ﻌ•^ that nyegates bevy's fast compiwe times, ^•ﻌ•^ and can b-be vewy annoying w-whiwe you devewop.

with the advice at the top of this p-page, OwO you don't n-nyeed to buiwd w-with --release, ^•ﻌ•^ just to test youw game with adequate p-pewfowmance. OwO y-you can use it fow actuaw wewease buiwds that you send to y-youw usews.

if you want, OwO you can awso enabwe w-wto (wink-time-optimization) f-fow t-the actuaw wewease buiwds, OwO to squeeze out even m-mowe pewfowmance a-at the cost o-of vewy swow compiwe times:

wto = "thin"

ewwow adding function as system

you can sometimes get confusing awcane c-compiwew ewwows w-when you twy t-to add systems to youw bevy app.

the ewwows can wook wike this:

the twait bound `fow<'w, OwO 's, 't0> fn(bevy::pwewude::quewy<'w, 🥺 's, òωó (&'t0 p-pawam)) {my_system}: i-intosystem<(), o.O (), (U ᵕ U❁) _>` i-is nyot satisfied

this is caused by youw function having i-incompatibwe p-pawametews. OwO bevy c-can onwy accept speciaw types as system p-pawametews.

you might awso ewwows that wook wike t-this:

t-the twait `wowwdquewy` i-is nyot impwemented f-fow `component`

these ewwows awe caused by a mawfowmed q-quewy.

common beginnew mistakes

  • using &mut Commands (bevy 0.4 syntax) instead of Commands.
  • using Query<MyStuff> instead of Query<&MyStuff> ow Query<&mut MyStuff>.
  • using Query<&ComponentA, &ComponentB> instead of Query<(&ComponentA, &ComponentB)> (fowgetting the tupwe)
  • using youw wesouwce types diwectwy w-without Res ow ResMut.
  • using youw component types diwectwy w-without putting t-them in a Query.
  • using othew awbitwawy types in youw f-function.

note that Query<Entity> is cowwect, (ꈍᴗꈍ) because the entity id i-is speciaw; it is nyot a component.

suppowted types

onwy the fowwowing types awe suppowted a-as system p-pawametews:

(wist in api docs)

  • Commands: manipuwate the ecs using commands
  • Res<T>: shawed access to a wesouwce
  • ResMut<T>: excwusive (mutabwe) access to a wesouwce
  • Option<Res<T>>: shawed access to a wesouwce that m-may nyot exist
  • Option<ResMut<T>>: excwusive (mutabwe) access to a wesouwce that may n-nyot exist
  • Query<T, F = ()> (can contain tupwes of up to 15 t-types): access to entities and components
  • ParamSet (with up to 8 pawams): wesowve confwicts between incompatibwe system p-pawametews
  • Local<T>: data wocaw to the system
  • EventReader<T>: weceive events
  • EventWriter<T>: send events
  • Extract<T>: extwact stage onwy! XD T is a system pawametew type to access f-fwom the main w-wowwd
  • RemovedComponents<T>: wemovaw detection
  • NonSend<T>: shawed access to non-Send (main thwead onwy) data
  • NonSendMut<T>: mut access to non-Send (main thwead onwy) data
  • ParallelCommands: abstwaction to hewp use Commands when you wiww do youw own pawawwewism
  • &World: wead-onwy diwect access to the ecs wowwd
  • Entities: wow-wevew ecs metadata: aww entities
  • Components: wow-wevew ecs metadata: aww components
  • Bundles: wow-wevew ecs metadata: aww bundwes
  • Archetypes: wow-wevew ecs metadata: aww awchetypes
  • SystemChangeTick: wow-wevew ecs metadata: tick used f-fow change detection
  • tupwes containing any of these types, ^•ﻌ•^ w-with up to 16 m-membews

youw function can have a maximum o-of 16 totaw pawametews. OwO i-if you need m-mowe, gwoup them into tupwes to wowk awound t-the wimit. OwO t-tupwes can contain u-up to 16 membews, >_< but can be nyested indefinitewy.

2d objects nyot dispwaying

bevy's 2d coowdinate space is set up so that youw backgwound c-can be at z=0.0, ^•ﻌ•^ and othew 2d objects c-can be wayewed a-at positive +z coowdinates above that.

thewefowe, OwO to see youw scene, 🥺 the c-camewa nyeeds to b-be pwaced faw a-away, òωó at a wawge +z coowdinate, >_< wooking towawds -z.

if you awe ovewwiding the camewa twansfowm / cweating youw own twansfowm, XD you nyeed to do this! the defauwt twansfowm (with z=0.0) wiww pwace the camewa so that youw s-spwites (at positive +z c-coowdinates) wouwd be behind the camewa, OwO and you w-wouwdn't see t-them! 🥺 you nyeed t-to eithew set a wawge z coowdinate, o-ow pwesewve/copy t-the z vawue fwom t-the Transform that is genewated by bevy's buiwtin b-bundwe constwuctow (Camera2dBundle::default()).

by defauwt, ^•ﻌ•^ when you cweate a 2d c-camewa using bevy's b-buiwt-in bundwe constwuctow, >< bevy sets the camewa Transform to have z=999.9. >< this is cwose to the defauwt cwipping pwane (visibwe w-wange of z axis), OwO w-which is set t-to 1000.0.

this wist is nyot exhaustive. OwO thewe m-may be othew u-unsuppowted scenawios t-that i did nyot know of ow fowgot to incwude h-hewe. (ꈍᴗꈍ) :)

ow bettew, OwO make suwe to spawn the p-pawent entities c-cowwectwy in the f-fiwst pwace. you can use a VisibilityBundle ow SpatialBundle (with twansfowms) if you awe nyot using a bundwe that awweady i-incwudes these c-components.

bowwow muwtipwe fiewds fwom stwuct

when you have a component ow wesouwce, XD that is wawgew stwuct with muwtipwe fiewds, OwO s-sometimes you w-want to bowwow s-sevewaw of the fiewds at the same time, (ꈍᴗꈍ) possibwy m-mutabwy.

    a: foo, rawr x3
    b-b: baw, rawr

    f-fow thing i-in q.itew_mut() {
        h-hewpew_func(&thing.a, &mut t-thing.b); // e-ewwow! σωσ

    // do something

this can wesuwt in a compiwew ewwow a-about confwicting b-bowwows:

ewwow[e0502]: cannot bowwow `thing` a-as mutabwe because i-it is awso b-bowwowed as immutabwe

    |         h-hewpew_func(&thing.a, σωσ &mut t-thing.b); // e-ewwow! >_<
    |         -----------  -----         ^^^^^ m-mutabwe b-bowwow occuws hewe
    |         |            |
    |         |            immutabwe bowwow occuws hewe
    |         immutabwe b-bowwow watew used by caww

the sowution is to use the "webowwow" i-idiom, 🥺 a common b-but nyon-obvious t-twick in wust p-pwogwamming:

note that this wine twiggews change detection. XD even if you don't modify the data aftewwawds, OwO t-the component g-gets mawked as c-changed.

expwanation

bevy typicawwy gives you access to y-youw data via s-speciaw wwappew t-types (wike Res<T>, rawr x3 ResMut<T>, XD and Mut<T> (when quewying fow components mutabwy)). (ꈍᴗꈍ) this wets b-bevy twack access to the data.

these awe "smawt pointew" types that u-use the wust Deref twait to dewefewence to youw data. OwO t-they usuawwy wowk s-seamwesswy and y-you don't even nyotice them.

howevew, ^•ﻌ•^ in a sense, OwO they awe opaque t-to the compiwew. 🥺 t-the wust wanguage awwows fiewds of a stwuct to be bowwowed i-individuawwy, OwO w-when you have d-diwect access to the stwuct, OwO but this does n-nyot wowk when i-it is wwapped i-in anothew type.

the "webowwow" twick shown above, ^•ﻌ•^ e-effectivewy convewts t-the wwappew into a weguwaw wust wefewence. >< *thing dewefewences the wwappew via DerefMut, XD and then &mut bowwows it mutabwy. >< you nyow have &mut MyStuff instead of Mut<MyStuff>.

bevy time vs. >_< wust/os time

do not use std::time::Instant::now() to get the cuwwent time. XD get youw timing infowmation fwom b-bevy, XD using Res<Time>.

wust (and the os) give you the pwecise t-time of the m-moment you caww t-that function. (ꈍᴗꈍ) howevew, ^•ﻌ•^ that's nyot nyani y-you want.

youw game systems awe wun by bevy's p-pawawwew scheduwew, OwO w-which means t-that they couwd be cawwed at vastwy diffewent i-instants evewy f-fwame! OwO this wiww w-wesuwt in inconsistent / jittewy timings and m-make youw game m-misbehave ow wook s-stuttewy.

bevy's Time gives you timing infowmation that i-is consistent thwoughout the fwame update cycwe. OwO i-it is intended t-to be used fow g-game wogic.

this is nyot bevy-specific, OwO but appwies t-to game devewopment i-in genewaw. 🥺 a-awways get youw time fwom youw game engine, OwO n-nyot fwom youw p-pwogwamming wanguage o-ow opewating system.

uv coowdinates in bevy

in bevy, OwO the vewticaw axis fow the p-pixews of textuwes / i-images, 🥺 and w-when sampwing textuwes in a shadew, >< points downwawds, >< fwom top to bottom. (ꈍᴗꈍ) the owigin is at the top weft.

this is inconsistent with the wowwd-coowdinate system used evewywhewe ewse in bevy, >_< whewe the y axis points up.

it is, OwO howevew, consistent with how m-most image fiwe f-fowmats stowe p-pixew data, and with how most gwaphics apis wowk (incwuding diwectx, ^•ﻌ•^ v-vuwkan, OwO m-metaw, webgpu, XD but not opengw).

opengw (and fwamewowks based on it) i-is diffewent. ^•ﻌ•^ i-if youw pwiow expewience is with that, ^•ﻌ•^ you may find that youw t-textuwes appeaw f-fwipped vewticawwy.

if you awe using a mesh, OwO make suwe i-it has the cowwect u-uv vawues. 🥺 i-if it was cweated with othew softwawe, ^•ﻌ•^ be suwe t-to sewect the c-cowwect settings.

if you awe wwiting a custom shadew, OwO m-make suwe youw u-uv awithmetic i-is cowwect.

coowdinate system

2d and 3d scenes and camewas

bevy uses a wight-handed y-up coowdinate s-system.

bevy uses the same coowdinate system f-fow 3d and 2d, ^•ﻌ•^ f-fow consistency.

it is easiest to expwain in tewms o-of 2d:

  • the x axis goes fwom weft to wight (+x p-points wight).
  • the y axis goes fwom bottom to top (+y p-points up).
  • the z axis goes fwom faw to nyeaw (+z p-points towawds y-you, OwO out of t-the scween).
  • fow 2d, (ꈍᴗꈍ) the owigin (x=0.0; y=0.0) i-is at the centew of the scween by defauwt.

when you awe wowking with 2d spwites, OwO y-you can put t-the backgwound o-on z=0.0, and pwace othew spwites at incweasing p-positive z coowdinates t-to wayew t-them on top.

in 3d, (ꈍᴗꈍ) the axes awe owiented the s-same way:

  • y points up
  • the fowwawd diwection is -z

this is a wight-handed coowdinate s-system. OwO you can u-use the fingews o-of youw wight hand to visuawize the 3 axes: thumb=x, (ꈍᴗꈍ) i-index=y, ^•ﻌ•^ middwe=z.

it is the same as godot, OwO maya, and o-opengw. 🥺 compawed t-to unity, òωó the z-z axis is invewted.

(gwaphic modifed and used with pewmission; o-owiginaw b-by @fweyahowmew)

awso bewawe of a common pitfaww when w-wowking in 2d: the camewa must be positioned at a faw away z coowdinate (=999.9 b-by d-defauwt), OwO ow you m-might nyot be abwe to see youw spwites!

ui

fow ui, OwO bevy fowwows the same convention a-as most o-othew ui toowkits, 🥺 t-the web, òωó etc.

  • the owigin is at the top weft cownew o-of the scween
  • the y axis points downwawds
  • x goes fwom 0.0 (weft scween edge) t-to the nyumbew o-of scween pixews (wight s-scween e-edge)
  • y goes fwom 0.0 (top scween edge) t-to the nyumbew o-of scween pixews (bottom s-scween e-edge)

the units wepwesent wogicaw (compensated f-fow dpi s-scawing) scween p-pixews.

ui wayout fwows fwom top to bottom, ^•ﻌ•^ s-simiwaw to a w-web page.

wogging, >_< consowe messages

you may have nyoticed how, OwO when you w-wun youw bevy p-pwoject, 🥺 you get m-messages in youw consowe window. >_< fow exampwe:

bevy offews a wogging fwamewowk that i-is much mowe a-advanced than simpwy u-using println/eprintln fwom wust. ^•ﻌ•^ wog messages can have m-metadata, OwO wike t-the wevew, OwO timestamp, 🥺 and wust moduwe w-whewe it came fwom. òωó y-you can see t-that this metadata is pwinted awongside the c-contents of the m-message.

wevews

wevews detewmine how impowtant a m-message is, OwO and a-awwow messages to b-be fiwtewed.

the avaiwabwe wevews awe: error, rawr x3 warn, rawr x3 info, rawr x3 debug, rawr x3 trace.

a wough guidewine fow when to use e-each wevew, ^•ﻌ•^ couwd b-be:

  • error: something happened that pwevents t-things fwom wowking c-cowwectwy
  • warn: something unusuaw happened, ^•ﻌ•^ but t-things can continue t-to wowk
  • info: genewaw infowmationaw messages
  • debug: fow devewopment, ^•ﻌ•^ messages about n-nyani youw code i-is doing
  • trace: fow vewy vewbose debug data, (ꈍᴗꈍ) wike d-dumping vawues

pwinting youw own wog messages

to dispway a message, OwO just use the m-macwo nyamed aftew t-the wevew of t-the message. (ꈍᴗꈍ) the syntax is exactwy the s-same as with wust's println. XD see the std::fmt documentation fow mowe detaiws.

fiwtewing messages

bevy asset management

assets awe the data that the game e-engine is wowking w-with: aww of y-youw images, 3d modews, ^•ﻌ•^ sounds, OwO scenes, game-specific t-things wike i-item descwiptions, and mowe!

bevy has a fwexibwe system fow woading a-and managing y-youw game assets asynchwonouswy (in the backgwound, ^•ﻌ•^ without causing w-wag spikes in y-youw game).

in youw code, (ꈍᴗꈍ) you wefew to individuaw a-assets using handwes.

asset data can be woaded fwom fiwes and awso accessed fwom code. rawr x3 hot-wewoading is suppowted to hewp you duwing devewopment, OwO by wewoading a-asset fiwes i-if they change w-whiwe the game is wunning.

if you want to wwite some code to d-do something when a-assets finish w-woading, get modified, (ꈍᴗꈍ) ow awe unwoaded, ^•ﻌ•^ you can u-use asset events.

handwes

handwes awe wightweight ids that w-wefew to a specific a-asset. OwO you need t-them to use youw assets, >_< fow exampwe to spawn entities wike 2d spwites ow 3d modews, XD ow to access the data of the assets.

handwes have the wust type Handle<T>, XD whewe T is the asset type.

you can stowe handwes in youw entity components ow wesouwces.

handwes can wefew to nyot-yet-woaded a-assets, OwO meaning y-you can just s-spawn youw entities anyway, using the handwes, OwO a-and the assets w-wiww just "pop i-in" when they become weady.

obtaining handwes

if you awe woading an asset fwom a fiwe, XD the asset_server.load(…) caww wiww give you the handwe. (ꈍᴗꈍ) the w-woading of the data happens in the backgwound, OwO meaning t-that the h-handwe wiww initiawwy w-wefew to an unavaiwabwe asset, OwO and the a-actuaw data wiww b-become avaiwabwe w-watew.

if you awe cweating youw own asset data fwom c-code, the assets.add(…) caww wiww give you the handwe.

wefewence counting; stwong and weak h-handwes

bevy keeps twack of how many handwes t-to a given asset e-exist at any t-time. OwO bevy wiww automaticawwy unwoad unused a-assets, OwO aftew the w-wast handwe is d-dwopped.

fow this weason, cweating additionaw h-handwes to the s-same asset wequiwes y-you to caww handle.clone(). ^•ﻌ•^ this makes the opewation expwicit, OwO t-to ensuwe you a-awe awawe of aww the pwaces in youw code w-whewe you cweate a-additionaw h-handwes. OwO the .clone() opewation is cheap, ^•ﻌ•^ so don't wowwy a-about pewfowmance (in m-most cases).

thewe awe two kinds of handwes: "stwong" a-and "weak". OwO s-stwong assets a-awe counted, OwO weak handwes awe nyot. 🥺 by d-defauwt, òωó handwes a-awe stwong. o.O if y-you want to cweate a weak handwe, >_< use .clone_weak() (instead of .clone()) on an existing handwe. bevy can unwoad t-the asset aftew a-aww stwong handwes a-awe gone, even if you awe stiww howding some w-weak handwes.

untyped handwes

bevy awso has a HandleUntyped type. XD use this type of handwe if you nyeed to be abwe t-to wefew to any a-asset, OwO wegawdwess o-of the asset type.

this awwows you to stowe a cowwection (such a-as Vec ow HashMap) containing assets of mixed types.

just wike weguwaw handwes, ^•ﻌ•^ untyped h-handwes can be s-stwong ow weak.

you can convewt an untyped handwe i-into a typed handwe w-with .typed::<T>(), specifying the type to use. (ꈍᴗꈍ) you need t-to do this to access the asset data.

whewe awe assets woaded fwom?

the asset sewvew intewnawwy wewies o-on an impwementation o-of the AssetIo wust twait, (ꈍᴗꈍ) which is bevy's way o-of pwoviding "backends" fow fetching data fwom d-diffewent types o-of stowage.

bevy pwovides its own defauwt buiwt-in i-i/o backends f-fow each suppowted pwatfowm.

on desktop pwatfowms, OwO it tweats asset p-paths as wewative t-to a fowdew c-cawwed assets, (ꈍᴗꈍ) that must be pwaced at one of the f-fowwowing wocations:

  • awongside the game's executabwe fiwe, (ꈍᴗꈍ) f-fow distwibution
  • in youw cawgo pwoject fowdew, ^•ﻌ•^ when w-wunning youw game u-using cargo duwing devewopment

key codes and scan codes

key codes wepwesent the symbow/wettew o-on each key a-and awe dependent o-on the keyboawd wayout cuwwentwy active i-in the usew's os. OwO b-bevy wepwesents t-them with the KeyCode enum.

wayout-agnostic key bindings

you couwd twy to pwovide a bettew e-expewience fow p-pwayews, OwO wegawdwess o-of these wimitations, XD by:

bevy assigns a unique id (Gamepad) to each connected gamepad. OwO this wets you associate t-the device with a-a specific pwayew a-and distinguish which one youw inputs a-awe coming fwom.

you can use the Gamepads wesouwce to wist the ids of aww the cuwwentwy connected g-gamepad devices, OwO o-ow to check t-the status of a specific one.

/// w-we nyeed to know w-which gamepad t-to use fow pwayew i-input. mya

fn gamepad_connections(
    mut commands: commands, 🥺
    my_gamepad: option<wes<mygamepad>>, >_<
    m-mut gamepad_evw: eventweadew<gamepadevent>, >_<
) {

        wet id = ev.gamepad;
        match &ev.event_type {
            gamepadeventtype::connected(info) => {
                p-pwintwn!("new gamepad c-connected with i-id: {:?}, (⑅˘꒳˘) nyame: {}", /(^•ω•^) id, info.name);

                // if we don't have any gamepad yet, rawr x3 use t-this one

                    commands.insewt_wesouwce(mygamepad(id));
                }
            }
            gamepadeventtype::disconnected => {
                pwintwn!("wost g-gamepad connection with id: {:?}", (U ﹏ U) i-id);

                // i-if it's t-the one we pweviouswy a-associated with the pwayew, (U ﹏ U)
                // disassociate i-it:

handwing gamepad inputs

you can handwe the anawog sticks a-and twiggews with Axis<GamepadAxis> (Axis, rawr x3 GamepadAxis). XD buttons can be handwed with Input<GamepadButton> (Input, GamepadButton), XD simiwaw to mouse buttons ow keyboawd keys.

fn gamepad_input(
    axes: wes<axis<gamepadaxis>>, òωó
    b-buttons: w-wes<input<gamepadbutton>>, ʘwʘ
    my_gamepad: o-option<wes<mygamepad>>, /(^•ω•^)
) {
    w-wet gamepad = i-if wet s-some(gp) = my_gamepad {
        // a-a gamepad is c-connected, ʘwʘ we have the id
        gp.0
    } ewse {

        wetuwn;
    };

    wet axis_wx = gamepadaxis {
        g-gamepad, σωσ axis_type: gamepadaxistype::weftstickx
    };
    wet axis_wy = g-gamepadaxis {
        gamepad, OwO a-axis_type: g-gamepadaxistype::weftsticky
    };

    if wet (some(x), 😳😳😳 some(y)) = (axes.get(axis_wx), 😳😳😳 axes.get(axis_wy)) {
        // combine x-x and y into one vectow
        wet weft_stick_pos = vec2::new(x, o.O y);

        // e-exampwe: check if the stick is p-pushed up
        i-if weft_stick_pos.wength() > 0.9 && w-weft_stick_pos.y > 0.5 {
            // d-do something
        }
    }

    w-wet jump_button = gamepadbutton {

    };

        g-gamepad, >w< button_type: gamepadbuttontype::east
    };

    i-if b-buttons.just_pwessed(jump_button) {
        // b-button just pwessed: make the pwayew jump
    }

        // b-button being hewd d-down: heaw the pwayew
    }
}

fn gamepad_input_events(
    my_gamepad: o-option<wes<mygamepad>>, rawr x3
    m-mut gamepad_evw: e-eventweadew<gamepadevent>, mya
) {
    w-wet gamepad = i-if wet some(gp) = m-my_gamepad {
        // a-a gamepad is connected, nyaa~~ w-we have the id
        gp.0

            continue;

                // w-wight stick moved (x)
            }
            axischanged(gamepadaxistype::wightsticky, (✿oωo) y) => {
                // wight stick moved (y)
            }
            b-buttonchanged(gamepadbuttontype::dpaddown, (ˆ ﻌ ˆ)♡ vaw) => {
                // buttons awe awso wepowted as anawog, (˘ω˘) so u-use a thweshowd

            _ => {} // d-don't c-cawe about othew i-inputs

}

quick-stawt: spawning 3d modews into y-youw wowwd

"3d modews" can often be compwex, OwO c-consisting of muwtipwe p-pawts. 🥺 think o-of a house: the windows, OwO woof, doows, e-etc., awe sepawate p-pieces, 🥺 that a-awe wikewy made of muwtipwe meshes, ^•ﻌ•^ matewiaws, OwO a-and textuwes. 🥺 b-bevy wouwd technicawwy need muwtipwe ecs entities to wepwesent a-and wendew t-the whowe thing.

intwoduction to gwtf

gwtf is a modewn open standawd fow e-exchanging 3d a-assets between diffewent 3d softwawe appwications, ^•ﻌ•^ wike game e-engines and 3d m-modewing softwawe.

the gwtf fiwe fowmat has two vawiants: h-human-weadabwe a-ascii/text (*.gltf) and binawy (*.glb). (ꈍᴗꈍ) the binawy fowmat is mowe compact a-and pwefewabwe fow packaging the assets with youw g-game. OwO the text f-fowmat may be usefuw f-fow devewopment, OwO as it can be easiew t-to manuawwy inspect u-using a text e-editow.

a gwtf fiwe can contain many objects (sub-assets): m-meshes, (ꈍᴗꈍ) matewiaws, textuwes, OwO scenes, 🥺 animation cwips. òωó w-when woading a g-gwtf fiwe, bevy w-wiww woad aww of the assets contained inside. ^•ﻌ•^ t-they wiww be m-mapped to the appwopwiate bevy-intewnaw asset types.

the gwtf sub-assets

gwtf tewminowogy can be confusing, OwO a-as it sometimes u-uses the same w-wowds to wefew to diffewent things, OwO compawed t-to bevy. 🥺 this s-section wiww twy e-expwain the vawious gwtf tewms.

to undewstand evewything, OwO it hewps t-to mentawwy considew h-how these c-concepts awe wepwesented in diffewent pwaces: i-in youw 3d modewing s-softwawe (wike b-bwendew), in the gwtf fiwe itsewf, >_< and in bevy.

gwtf scenes awe nyani you spawn into youw game w-wowwd. ^•ﻌ•^ this is t-typicawwy nani you see on the scween in youw 3d m-modewing softwawe. ^•ﻌ•^ s-scenes combine aww of the data needed fow the game e-engine to cweate a-aww the nyeeded entities to wepwesent nyani you want. OwO c-conceptuawwy, 🥺 t-think of a scene a-as one "unit". ^•ﻌ•^ depending on youw use case, OwO t-this couwd be o-one "3d modew", ow even a whowe map ow game wevew. OwO i-in bevy, these a-awe wepwesented a-as bevy scenes with aww the chiwd ecs entities.

gwtf scenes awe composed of gwtf nodes. >_< these descwibe the "objects" in the scene, OwO typicawwy gwtf meshes, 🥺 b-but can awso b-be othew things w-wike camewas and wights. OwO each gwtf nyode h-has a twansfowm f-fow positioning i-it in the scene. OwO gwtf nodes do nyot have a-a cowe bevy equivawent; b-bevy just u-uses this data to cweate the ecs entities i-inside of a s-scene. OwO bevy has a-a speciaw GltfNode asset type, (ꈍᴗꈍ) if you nyeed access t-to this data.

gwtf meshes wepwesent one conceptuaw "3d object". (ꈍᴗꈍ) t-these cowwespond to the "objects" in youw 3d modewing s-softwawe. gwtf m-meshes may be c-compwex and composed of muwtipwe smowew pieces, OwO c-cawwed gwtf p-pwimitives, 🥺 each o-of which may use a diffewent matewiaw. OwO g-gwtf meshes do n-nyot have a cowe b-bevy equivawent, >_< but thewe is a speciaw GltfMesh asset type, which descwibes the pwimitives.

gwtf pwimitives awe individuaw "units of 3d geometwy", ^•ﻌ•^ f-fow the puwposes o-of wendewing. OwO they contain the actuaw g-geometwy / vewtex d-data, 🥺 and wefewence t-the matewiaw to be used when dwawing. OwO i-in bevy, each gwtf p-pwimitive is w-wepwesented as a bevy Mesh asset, (ꈍᴗꈍ) and must be spawned as a s-sepawate ecs entity to be wendewed.

gwtf matewiaws descwibe the shading pawametews f-fow the suwfaces o-of youw 3d modews. ^•ﻌ•^ they have fuww suppowt f-fow physicawwy-based w-wendewing (pbw). OwO they awso wefewence the textuwes t-to use. 🥺 in b-bevy, they awe w-wepwesented as StandardMaterial assets, >_< as used by the bevy pbw 3d wendewew.

gwtf textuwes (images) can be embedded inside t-the gwtf fiwe, ^•ﻌ•^ ow s-stowed extewnawwy in sepawate image fiwes a-awongside it. OwO f-fow exampwe, 🥺 you c-can have youw textuwes as sepawate png/jpeg/ktx2 f-fiwes fow e-ease of devewopment, OwO o-ow package them aww inside the gwtf f-fiwe fow ease of d-distwibution. OwO in b-bevy, gwtf textuwes awe woaded as bevy Image assets.

gwtf sampwews descwibe the settings fow how the g-gpu shouwd use a-a given textuwe. ^•ﻌ•^ bevy does nyot keep t-these sepawate; t-this data is stowed inside the bevy Image asset (the sampler fiewd of type SamplerDescriptor).

gwtf animations descwibe animations that intewpowate v-vawious vawues, such as twansfowms ow mesh skewetons, OwO o-ovew time. 🥺 i-in bevy, these awe w-woaded as AnimationClip assets.

gwtf usage pattewns

a singwe gwtf fiwe can contain any n-nyumbew of sub-assets o-of any of t-the above types, (ꈍᴗꈍ) wefewwing to each othew howevew t-they wike.

  • to wepwesent sections of a wevew/map, OwO s-such as a wooms, 🥺 a-as sepawate g-gwtf scenes. they can shawe meshes and textuwes i-if nyeeded.
  • to contain a set of many diffewent "3d m-modews", OwO each a-as a sepawate g-gwtf scene. this wets you woad and manage the w-whowe cowwection a-at once and spawn t-them individuawwy a-as nyeeded.
  • … othews?

this is anothew way to access specific s-sub-assets. ^•ﻌ•^ i-it is wess wewiabwe, but may be easiew to use in some c-cases.

the fowwowing asset wabews awe suppowted ({} is the nyumewicaw index):

  • Scene{}: gwtf scene as bevy Scene
  • Node{}: gwtf nyode as GltfNode
  • Mesh{}: gwtf mesh as GltfMesh
  • Mesh{}/Primitive{}: gwtf pwimitive as bevy Mesh
  • Texture{}: gwtf textuwe as bevy Image
  • Material{}: gwtf matewiaw as bevy StandardMaterial
  • DefaultMaterial: as above, OwO if the gwtf fiwe contains a-a defauwt matewiaw w-with nyo i-index
  • Animation{}: gwtf animation as bevy AnimationClip
  • Skin{}: gwtf mesh skin as bevy SkinnedMeshInverseBindposes

the GltfNode and GltfMesh asset types awe onwy usefuw to hewp y-you nyavigate t-the contents of youw gwtf fiwe. OwO they awe nyot cowe b-bevy wendewew t-types, 🥺 and nyot u-used by bevy in any othew way. ^•ﻌ•^ the bevy w-wendewew expects e-entities with MaterialMeshBundle; fow that you nyeed the Mesh and StandardMaterial.

bevy wimitations

bevy does nyot fuwwy suppowt aww f-featuwes of the g-gwtf fowmat and h-has some specific wequiwements about the data. OwO n-nyot aww gwtf f-fiwes can be w-woaded and wendewed in bevy. OwO unfowtunatewy, i-in many of these c-cases, 🥺 you wiww n-nyot get any ewwow ow diagnostic message.

commonwy-encountewed wimitations:

  • textuwes embedded in ascii (*.gltf) fiwes (base64 encoding) cannot b-be woaded. put youw textuwes in extewnaw fiwes, (ꈍᴗꈍ) o-ow use the binawy (*.glb) fowmat.
  • mipmaps awe onwy suppowted if the t-textuwe fiwes (in k-ktx2 ow dds fowmat) c-contain them. the gwtf spec wequiwes missing mipmap d-data to be g-genewated by the g-game engine, 🥺 but b-bevy does nyot suppowt this yet. 🥺 if youw a-assets awe missing m-mipmaps, òωó textuwes w-wiww wook g-gwainy/noisy.

this wist is nyot exhaustive. OwO thewe m-may be othew u-unsuppowted scenawios t-that i did nyot know of ow fowgot to incwude h-hewe. (ꈍᴗꈍ) :)

bevy pwogwamming fwamewowk

this chaptew pwesents the featuwes o-of the bevy cowe p-pwogwamming fwamewowk. OwO t-this covews the ecs (entity component s-system), ^•ﻌ•^ app and s-scheduwing.

ecs as a data stwuctuwe

wewevant officiaw exampwes: ecs_guide.

awso check out the compwete game e-exampwes: alien_cake_addict, breakout.

bevy stowes and manages aww youw d-data fow you, using t-the bevy ecs (entity-component system).

conceptuawwy, OwO you can think of it b-by anawogy with t-tabwes, 🥺 wike in a-a database ow spweadsheet. ^•ﻌ•^ youw diffewent data t-types (components) a-awe wike the "cowumns" of a tabwe, (ꈍᴗꈍ) and thewe can be awbitwawiwy m-many "wows" (entities) containing vawues / instances of vawious components.

fow exampwe, >< you couwd cweate a Health component fow youw game. >< you couwd then have many entities wepwesenting d-diffewent things i-in youw game, OwO s-such as the pwayew, ^•ﻌ•^ nypcs, OwO ow monstews, 🥺 a-aww of which can h-have a Health vawue (as weww as othew wewevant components).

this makes it easy to wwite game w-wogic (systems) that can opewate on any entity with the nyecessawy c-components (such a-as a heawth/damage system fow anything that has Health), >_< wegawdwess of whethew that's the pwayew, OwO an nypc, ow a monstew (ow a-anything ewse). 🥺 t-this makes youw g-game wogic vewy fwexibwe and weusabwe.

the set / combination of components t-that a given e-entity has, is cawwed t-the entity's awchetype.

note that entities awen't wimited t-to just "objects i-in the game wowwd". OwO t-the ecs is a genewaw-puwpose data stwuctuwe. OwO y-you can cweate e-entities and c-components to stowe any data.

pewfowmance

bevy has a smawt scheduwing awgowithm t-that wuns youw s-systems in pawawwew as much as possibwe. OwO it does that a-automaticawwy, 🥺 w-when youw functions d-don't wequiwe confwicting access to the s-same data. OwO youw g-game wiww scawe t-to wun on muwtipwe cpu cowes "fow fwee"; that i-is, ^•ﻌ•^ without wequiwing e-extwa devewopment effowt fwom you.

to impwove the chances fow pawawwewism, OwO y-you can make y-youw data and c-code mowe gwanuwaw. (ꈍᴗꈍ) spwit youw data into smowew t-types / structs. XD spwit youw wogic into muwtipwe smowew systems / functions. OwO h-have each s-system access o-onwy the data that is wewevant to it. OwO the f-fewew access confwicts, 🥺 t-the fastew y-youw game wiww wun.

the genewaw wuwe of thumb fow bevy p-pewfowmance is: m-mowe gwanuwaw i-is bettew.

note fow pwogwammews coming fwom o-object-owiented w-wanguages

you may be used to thinking in tewms o-of "object cwasses". OwO f-fow exampwe, 🥺 y-you might be tempted to define a big m-monowithic struct Player containing aww the fiewds / pwopewties of the pwayew.

in bevy, OwO this is considewed bad pwactice, 🥺 b-because d-doing it that way c-can make it mowe difficuwt to wowk with youw d-data, ^•ﻌ•^ and wimit p-pewfowmance.

instead, OwO you shouwd make things gwanuwaw, 🥺 w-when diffewent p-pieces of d-data may be accessed independentwy.

fow exampwe, ^•ﻌ•^ wepwesent the pwayew i-in youw game as a-an entity, composed of sepawate component types (sepawate structs) fow things wike the heawth, ^•ﻌ•^ xp, ow nyanievew is wewevant t-to youw game. OwO y-you can awso attach standawd bevy components wike Transform (twansfowms expwained) to it.

this wiww make it easiew fow you t-to devewop youw s-systems (game wogic / behaviows), ^•ﻌ•^ as weww as make youw g-game's wuntime pewfowmance b-bettew.

howevew, >< something wike a Transform, XD ow a set of coowdinates, (ꈍᴗꈍ) stiww makes sense as a-a singwe struct, >< because its fiewds awe not wikewy to be usefuw independentwy.

wewevant officiaw exampwes: ecs_guide.

entities

entities awe just a simpwe integew id, (ꈍᴗꈍ) that identifies a pawticuwaw set o-of component vawues.

to cweate ("spawn") nyew entities, (ꈍᴗꈍ) u-use Commands.

components

components awe the data associated w-with entities.

to cweate a nyew component type, s-simpwy define a w-wust struct ow enum, XD and dewive the Component twait.

#[dewive(component)]
stwuct heawth {
    hp: f32, (ꈍᴗꈍ)
    e-extwa: f32, ^•ﻌ•^
}

types must be unique -- an entity c-can onwy have one c-component pew w-wust type.

use wwappew (newtype) stwucts to m-make unique components o-out of simpwew t-types:

#[dewive(component)]

you can use empty stwucts to hewp y-you identify specific e-entities. OwO t-these awe known as "mawkew components". (ꈍᴗꈍ) usefuw w-with quewy fiwtews.

#[dewive(component)]

/// this w-wiww be used to identify the main pwayew entity
#[dewive(component)]
stwuct pwayew;

/// tag aww c-cweatuwes that awe cuwwentwy fwiendwy towawds t-the pwayew
#[dewive(component)]
stwuct fwiendwy;

components can be accessed fwom systems, XD using quewies.

you can add/wemove components on e-existing entities, ^•ﻌ•^ u-using Commands.

component bundwes

bundwes awe wike "tempwates", OwO to m-make it easy to c-cweate entities w-with a common set of components.

stwuct pwayewbundwe {
    xp: pwayewxp, rawr
    n-nyame: p-pwayewname, σωσ
    h-heawth: heawth, σωσ
    _p: p-pwayew, >_<

    // w-we can n-nyest/incwude a-anothew bundwe. :3
    // a-add the components fow a standawd bevy spwite:
    #[bundwe]
    spwite: spwitesheetbundwe, (U ﹏ U)
}

bevy awso considews awbitwawy tupwes o-of components a-as bundwes:

(componenta, >_< componentb, (ꈍᴗꈍ) componentc)

note that you cannot quewy fow a whowe bundwe. (ꈍᴗꈍ) bundwes awe j-just a convenience when cweating the entities. OwO q-quewy fow t-the individuaw c-component types that youw system nyeeds to access.

wesouwces

wewevant officiaw exampwes: ecs_guide.

wesouwces awwow you to stowe a singwe g-gwobaw instance o-of some data t-type, independentwy of entities.

use them fow data that is twuwy gwobaw f-fow youw app, ^•ﻌ•^ s-such as configuwation / settings.

to cweate a nyew wesouwce type, (ꈍᴗꈍ) simpwy d-define a wust struct ow enum, XD and dewive the Resource twait, XD simiwaw to components.

types must be unique; thewe can onwy b-be one instance o-of a given type.

#[dewive(wesouwce)]
stwuct goawsweached {
    main_goaw: b-boow,
    b-bonus: boow, ^•ﻌ•^
}

wesouwces can be accessed fwom systems, XD using Res/ResMut.

wesouwce initiawization

impw f-fwomwowwd fow myfancywesouwce {
    f-fn fwom_wowwd(wowwd: &mut w-wowwd) -> s-sewf {
        // y-you have f-fuww access to a-anything in the e-ecs fwom hewe. >_<
        // fow instance, :3 you can mutate othew wesouwces:
        wet mut x = wowwd.get_wesouwce_mut::<myothewwesouwce>().unwwap();
        x-x.do_mut_stuff();

        myfancywesouwce { /* stuff */ }

}

you can initiawize youw wesouwces a-at App cweation:

        // ...

        // if it impwements `defauwt` o-ow `fwomwowwd`

Commands can be used to cweate/wemove wesouwces f-fwom inside a system:

if you insewt a wesouwce of a type t-that awweady exists, OwO i-it wiww be o-ovewwwitten.

usage advice

the choice of when to use entities/components v-vs. ^•ﻌ•^ w-wesouwces is typicawwy about how you want to access the d-data: gwobawwy fwom a-anywhewe (wesouwces), ow using ecs pattewns (entities/components).

even if thewe is onwy one of a cewtain t-thing in youw g-game (such as t-the pwayew in a singwe-pwayew game), i-it can be a good f-fit to use an entity instead of wesouwces, ^•ﻌ•^ because entities a-awe composed o-of muwtipwe components, some of which can be common with o-othew entities. OwO t-this can make youw g-game wogic mowe fwexibwe. OwO fow exampwe, 🥺 y-you couwd have a-a "heawth/damage s-system" that wowks with both the pwayew and e-enemies.

systems

wewevant officiaw exampwes: ecs_guide, startup_system, system_param.

systems awe functions you wwite, w-which awe wun by b-bevy.

this is whewe you impwement aww youw g-game wogic.

these functions can onwy take speciaw pawametew types, to specify nyani you nyeed access t-to. (ꈍᴗꈍ) if you use unsuppowted pawametew t-types in youw function, ^•ﻌ•^ you wiww get confusing c-compiwew e-ewwows!

some of the options awe:

  • accessing wesouwces using Res/ResMut
  • accessing components of entities using quewies (Query)
  • cweating/destwoying entities, (ꈍᴗꈍ) components, ^•ﻌ•^ and wesouwces u-using commands (Commands)
  • sending/weceiving events using EventWriter/EventReader
fn debug_stawt(
    // access wesouwce
    s-stawt: w-wes<stawtingwevew>
) {
    e-epwintwn!("stawting o-on wevew {:?}", 🥺 *stawt);
}

system pawametews can be gwouped i-into tupwes (which c-can be nyested). OwO t-this is usefuw fow owganization.

    (a, UwU mut b): (wes<wesouwcea>, rawr x3 w-wesmut<wesouwceb>), rawr
    // t-this w-wesouwce might n-nyot exist, σωσ so w-wwap it in an option
    m-mut c: o-option<wesmut<wesouwcec>>, σωσ

        // do something
    }

youw function can have a maximum o-of 16 totaw pawametews. OwO i-if you need m-mowe, gwoup them into tupwes to wowk awound t-the wimit. OwO t-tupwes can contain u-up to 16 membews, >_< but can be nyested indefinitewy.

wuntime

as youw pwoject gwows mowe compwex, OwO y-you might want t-to enhance youw a-app buiwdew with some of the powewfuw toows that b-bevy offews f-fow managing when/how youw systems wun, >_< such as: expwicit owdewing with wabews, rawr x3 system sets, rawr x3 states, wun cwitewia, XD and stages.

quewies

wewevant officiaw exampwes: ecs_guide.

quewies wet you access components of entities.

fn check_zewo_heawth(
    // access e-entities that h-have `heawth` and `twansfowm` components
    // g-get wead-onwy access t-to `heawth` a-and mutabwe access t-to `twansfowm`
    // o-optionaw c-component: get access to `pwayew` if it exists
    mut quewy: quewy<(&heawth, rawr &mut t-twansfowm, OwO option<&pwayew>)>, (U ﹏ U)
) {
    // get aww matching e-entities
    fow (heawth, >_< mut twansfowm, rawr x3 p-pwayew) in quewy.itew_mut() {
        epwintwn!("entity at {} has {} hp.", mya t-twansfowm.twanswation, nyaa~~ heawth.hp);

        // c-centew if hp i-is zewo
        if heawth.hp <= 0.0 {
            twansfowm.twanswation = vec3::zewo;
        }

        if wet s-some(pwayew) = pwayew {
            // the cuwwent entity is the pwayew! (⑅˘꒳˘)
            // d-do something speciaw! rawr x3
        }
    }
}

get the components associated with a specific entity:

    if wet ok((heawth, ( ͡o ω ͡o ) mut twansfowm)) = q-quewy.get_mut(entity) {
        // d-do something w-with the c-components
    } e-ewse {
        // t-the entity does n-nyot have the c-components fwom the quewy
    }

get the ids (Entity) of the entities you access with youw quewies:

// add `entity` to `quewy` to get e-entity ids
fn quewy_entities(q: q-quewy<(entity, (U ᵕ U❁) /* ... */)>) {
    f-fow (e, (⑅˘꒳˘) /* ... */) i-in q.itew() {
        // `e` i-is the entity i-id of the entity w-we awe accessing
    }
}

if you know that the quewy shouwd o-onwy evew match a-a singwe entity, OwO y-you can use single/single_mut, XD instead of itewating:

    // d-do something w-with the pwayew a-and its twansfowm

(this wiww panic if the quewy matches m-mowe than one e-entity)

bundwes

quewies wowk with individuaw components. OwO i-if you cweated a-an entity u-using a bundwe, ^•ﻌ•^ you nyeed to quewy fow the specific c-components f-fwom that bundwe that you cawe about.

a common beginnew mistake is to quewy f-fow the bundwe t-type!

quewy fiwtews

add quewy fiwtews to nyawwow down t-the entities you g-get fwom the quewy.

fn debug_pwayew_hp(

    q-quewy: quewy<(&heawth, ^^;; o-option<&pwayewname>), >_< (with<pwayew>, mya w-without<enemy>)>, mya
) {

    fow (heawth, 😳 nyame) in quewy.itew() {
        i-if wet some(name) = name {

        } ewse {
            epwintwn!("unknown pwayew h-has {} hp.", 😳😳😳 heawth.hp);

muwtipwe fiwtews can be combined:

  • in a tupwe to appwy aww of them (and w-wogic)
  • using the Or<(…)> wwappew to detect any of them (ow w-wogic).

commands

wewevant officiaw exampwes: ecs_guide.

use Commands to spawn/despawn entities, >_< add/wemove components on existing entities, m-manage wesouwces.

these actions do nyot take effect i-immediatewy; they a-awe queued to b-be pewfowmed watew when it is safe to do so. >_< see: stages.

(if you awe nyot using stages, (ꈍᴗꈍ) that m-means youw othew systems wiww see them on the nyext fwame u-update)

fn spawn_things(
    mut commands: c-commands, mya
) {

    c-commands.insewt_wesouwce(goawsweached { m-main_goaw: fawse, 😳 b-bonus: fawse });

    // pwoviding the data fow the components it s-shouwd have
    // (typicawwy using a bundwe)
    commands.spawn(pwayewbundwe {
        n-nyame: pwayewname("henwy".into()),
        x-xp: pwayewxp(1000), 🥺
        heawth: heawth {
            hp: 100.0, o.O extwa: 20.0
        }, /(^•ω•^)
        _p: p-pwayew, nyaa~~
        spwite: d-defauwt::defauwt(), nyaa~~
    });

    // (tupwes o-of component and bundwe types awe considewed bundwes)
    // (note the extwa p-pawentheses)

        // a-add some components
        c-componenta, :3
        c-componentb::defauwt(), 😳😳😳

        m-mybundwe::defauwt(), (˘ω˘)
        twansfowmbundwe::defauwt(), ^^

        .insewt(componentc::defauwt())

f-fn make_aww_pwayews_hostiwe(
    m-mut commands: c-commands, -.-
    // we nyeed the entity id, 😳 to pewfowm commands o-on specific e-entities
    quewy: quewy<entity, mya w-with<pwayew>>, (˘ω˘)

            // add an `enemy` c-component to the entity

    m-mut commands: commands, >_<

events

wewevant officiaw exampwes: event.

send data between systems! >_< wet youw systems communicate with each othew!

  • to send events, >_< use an EventWriter<T>.
  • to weceive events, >_< use an EventReader<T>.

evewy weadew twacks the events it h-has wead independentwy, OwO s-so you c-can handwe the same events fwom muwtipwe systems.

stwuct wevewupevent(entity);

fn p-pwayew_wevew_up(
    m-mut ev_wevewup: e-eventwwitew<wevewupevent>, :3
    q-quewy: quewy<(entity, (U ﹏ U) &pwayewxp)>,
) {
    fow (entity, -.- x-xp) i-in quewy.itew() {
        i-if xp.0 > 1000 {
            e-ev_wevewup.send(wevewupevent(entity));
        }
    }
}

fn debug_wevewups(
    mut ev_wevewup: eventweadew<wevewupevent>, (ˆ ﻌ ˆ)♡
) {
    fow ev i-in ev_wevewup.itew() {
        epwintwn!("entity {:?} wevewed u-up!", (⑅˘꒳˘) ev.0);
    }
}

you nyeed to add youw custom event t-types via the app buiwdew:

fn main() {
    app::new()
        // ...
        .add_event::<wevewupevent>()
        .add_system(pwayew_wevew_up)
        .add_system(debug_wevewups)
        // ...
        .wun();
}

events shouwd be youw go-to data f-fwow toow. OwO as events c-can be sent f-fwom any system and weceived by muwtipwe systems, (ꈍᴗꈍ) t-they awe extwemewy vewsatiwe.

possibwe pitfawws

bewawe of fwame deway / 1-fwame-wag. ^•ﻌ•^ this can occuw i-if bevy wuns t-the weceiving system befowe the sending system. OwO t-the weceiving system w-wiww onwy g-get a chance to weceive the events on the nyext f-fwame update. OwO i-if you nyeed to e-ensuwe that events awe handwed immediatewy / d-duwing the same f-fwame, ^•ﻌ•^ you can use expwicit system owdewing.

events don't pewsist. OwO they awe stowed u-untiw the end o-of the nyext f-fwame, aftew which they awe wost. OwO if youw s-systems do nyot h-handwe events e-evewy fwame, you couwd miss some.

the advantage of this design is that y-you don't have t-to wowwy about e-excessive memowy use fwom unhandwed events.

if you don't wike this, >_< you can have manuaw contwow ovew w-when events awe cweawed (at the wisk of weaking / wasting m-memowy if you fowget to cweaw them).

app buiwdew (main function)

wewevant officiaw exampwes: aww of t-them ;)

in pawticuwaw, (ꈍᴗꈍ) check out the compwete g-game exampwes: alien_cake_addict, breakout.

to entew the bevy wuntime, ^•ﻌ•^ you nyeed t-to configuwe a-an App. XD the app is how you define the stwuctuwe of a-aww the things t-that make up youw p-pwoject: pwugins, rawr x3 systems, rawr x3 event types, states, rawr x3 stages…

technicawwy, XD the App contains the ecs wowwd(s) (whewe a-aww the data is stowed) and scheduwe(s) (whewe a-aww the systems to wun awe stowed). (ꈍᴗꈍ) fow advanced u-use-cases, ^•ﻌ•^ sub-apps awe a way to have mowe than one ecs wowwd a-and scheduwe.

wocaw wesouwces do nyot nyeed to be wegistewed. t-they awe pawt of theiw wespective systems.

component types do nyot nyeed to be wegistewed.

scheduwes cannot (yet) be modified a-at wuntime; aww systems you want to wun must be added/configuwed i-in the App ahead of time.

the data in the ecs wowwd can be m-modified at any t-time; cweate/destwoy y-youw entities and wesouwces, XD fwom systems using commands, XD ow excwusive systems using diwect wowwd access.

wesouwces can awso be initiawized ahead of t-time, (ꈍᴗꈍ) hewe in the App buiwdew.

you awso nyeed to add the pwugin gwoup with bevy's buiwt-in functionawity: eithew DefaultPlugins if you awe making a fuww game/app, (ꈍᴗꈍ) o-ow MinimalPlugins fow something wike a headwess sewvew.

note that thewe awe some speciaw configuwation wesouwces that must be added fiwst, OwO if you w-wouwd wike to use t-them, 🥺 to take e-effect.

fn main() {
    app::new()
        // bevy itsewf:
        .add_pwugins(defauwtpwugins)

        // w-wesouwces:
        .insewt_wesouwce(stawtingwevew(3))

        // e-events:
        .add_event::<wevewupevent>()

        .add_stawtup_system(spawn_things)

        // s-systems to w-wun each fwame:
        .add_system(pwayew_wevew_up)
        .add_system(debug_wevewups)
        .add_system(debug_stats_change)
        // ...

        .wun();

quitting the app

to cweanwy shut down bevy, >_< send an AppExit event fwom any system:

    e-exit.send(appexit);
}

fow pwototyping, bevy pwovides a s-system you can add to youw App, to cwose the focused window on pwessing t-the Esc key. >< when aww windows awe cwosed, >< bevy wiww quit automaticawwy.

wocaw wesouwces

wewevant officiaw exampwes: ecs_guide.

wocaw wesouwces awwow you to have p-pew-system data.

Local<T> is a system pawametew simiwaw to ResMut<T>, (ꈍᴗꈍ) which gives you fuww mutabwe access t-to an instance of some data type, OwO that i-is independent fwom e-entities and c-components.

Res<T>/ResMut<T> wefew to a singwe gwobaw instance of the type, OwO shawed between a-aww systems. 🥺 o-on the othew hand, òωó e-evewy Local<T> pawametew is a sepawate instance, (ꈍᴗꈍ) e-excwusivewy fow that system.

#[dewive(defauwt)]
stwuct mystate;

fn my_system1(mut w-wocaw: wocaw<mystate>) {
    // y-you can do a-anything you want w-with the wocaw h-hewe
}

fn my_system2(mut w-wocaw: w-wocaw<mystate>) {
    // t-the wocaw in this system is a diffewent instance
}

the type must impwement Default ow FromWorld. >_< it is automaticawwy initiawized.

a system can have muwtipwe Locals of the same type.

specify an initiaw vawue

Local<T> is awways automaticawwy initiawized u-using the defauwt vawue fow the type.

if you nyeed specific data, ^•ﻌ•^ you can u-use a cwosuwe i-instead. OwO wust cwosuwes that take system pawametews awe vawid b-bevy systems, ^•ﻌ•^ j-just wike standawone functions. ^•ﻌ•^ using a cwosuwe awwows y-you to "move data i-into the function".

this exampwe shows how to initiawize s-some data to c-configuwe a system, without using Local<T>:

#[dewive(defauwt)]
stwuct myconfig {
    magic: usize, 😳
}

f-fn my_system(
    m-mut cmd: c-commands, XD
    m-my_wes: wes<mystuff>,
    // note t-this isn't a v-vawid system pawametew
    c-config: &myconfig, :3
) {
    // t-todo: do stuff
}

fn main() {
    wet config = myconfig {
        magic: 420, 😳😳😳
    };

    a-app::new()
        // cweate a "move cwosuwe", -.- s-so we can use the `config`
        // v-vawiabwe that we cweated above
        .add_system(move |cmd: commands, ( ͡o ω ͡o ) w-wes: wes<mystuff>| {
            // caww ouw function f-fwom inside t-the cwosuwe
            my_system(cmd, rawr x3 wes, &config);
        })
        .wun();
}

pwugins

wewevant officiaw exampwes: plugin, plugin_group.

as youw pwoject gwows, OwO it can be u-usefuw to make it m-mowe moduwaw. 🥺 y-you can spwit it into "pwugins".

pwugins awe simpwy cowwections of t-things to be added t-to the app buiwdew.

stwuct mypwugin;

    f-fn buiwd(&sewf, o.O a-app: &mut app) {
        a-app
            .init_wesouwce::<myothewwesouwce>()
            .add_event::<myevent>()
            .add_stawtup_system(pwugin_init)

f-fn main() {
    a-app::new()
        .add_pwugins(defauwtpwugins)
        .add_pwugin(mypwugin)

fow intewnaw owganization in youw o-own pwoject, the m-main vawue of p-pwugins comes fwom nyot having to decwawe a-aww youw wust types a-and functions a-as pub, (ꈍᴗꈍ) just so they can be accessibwe f-fwom fn main to be added to the app buiwdew. (ꈍᴗꈍ) pwugins wet you add t-things to youw app fwom muwtipwe diffewent pwaces, (ꈍᴗꈍ) wike sepawate wust f-fiwes / moduwes.

you can decide how pwugins fit into t-the awchitectuwe o-of youw game.

some suggestions:

  • cweate pwugins fow diffewent states.
  • cweate pwugins fow vawious sub-systems, ^•ﻌ•^ w-wike physics o-ow input handwing.

pwugin gwoups

pwugin gwoups wegistew muwtipwe pwugins a-at once. bevy's DefaultPlugins and MinimalPlugins awe exampwes of this. to cweate youw own pwugin gwoup:

stwuct mypwugingwoup;

    fn b-buiwd(sewf) -> p-pwugingwoupbuiwdew {
        p-pwugingwoupbuiwdew::stawt::<sewf>()
            .add(foopwugin)
            .add(bawpwugin)
    }
}

f-fn main() {
    a-app::new()
        .add_pwugins(defauwtpwugins)
        .add_pwugins(mypwugingwoup)
        .wun();
}

when adding a pwugin gwoup to the app, >_< you can disabwe some pwugins whiwe keeping the west.

fow exampwe, ^•ﻌ•^ if you want to manuawwy s-set up wogging (with y-youw own tracing subscwibew), >_< you can disabwe bevy's LogPlugin:

    .add_pwugins(
        defauwtpwugins.buiwd()
            .disabwe::<wogpwugin>()
    )
    .wun();

note that this simpwy disabwes the f-functionawity, ^•ﻌ•^ b-but it cannot actuawwy wemove the code to avoid binawy bwoat. OwO t-the disabwed p-pwugins stiww h-have to be compiwed into youw pwogwam.

system owdew of execution

bevy's scheduwing awgowithm is designed t-to dewivew m-maximum pewfowmance by wunning as many systems as possibwe i-in pawawwew a-acwoss the avaiwabwe cpu thweads.

this is possibwe when the systems d-do nyot confwict o-ovew the data t-they nyeed to access. OwO howevew, 🥺 when a system n-nyeeds to have m-mutabwe (excwusive) a-access to a piece of data, OwO othew systems t-that nyeed to access t-the same data c-cannot be wun at the same time. OwO bevy detewmines a-aww of this i-infowmation f-fwom the system's function signatuwe (the t-types of the pawametews i-it takes).

in such situations, >< the owdew is nondetewministic by defauwt. >< bevy takes no wegawd fow when each system wiww w-wun, OwO and the o-owdew couwd even c-change evewy fwame!

does it even mattew?

in many cases, (ꈍᴗꈍ) you don't nyeed to w-wowwy about this.

howevew, OwO sometimes you nyeed to wewy o-on specific s-systems to wun in a-a pawticuwaw owdew. XD fow exampwe:

  • maybe the wogic you wwote in one o-of youw systems n-nyeeds any modifications done to that data by anothew system t-to awways happen f-fiwst?
  • one system nyeeds to weceive events sent by anothew system.
  • you awe using change detection.

in such situations, OwO systems wunning i-in the wwong o-owdew typicawwy c-causes theiw behaviow to be dewayed untiw t-the nyext fwame. OwO i-in wawe cases, 🥺 d-depending on youw game wogic, ^•ﻌ•^ it may even wesuwt i-in mowe sewious w-wogic bugs!

it is up to you to decide if this i-is impowtant.

with many things in typicaw games, OwO s-such as juicy v-visuaw effects, 🥺 i-it pwobabwy doesn't mattew if they get dewayed b-by a fwame. it m-might nyot be wowthwhiwe to bothew with it. OwO if you don't cawe, 🥺 w-weaving the o-owdew ambiguous m-may awso wesuwt in bettew pewfowmance.

on the othew hand, ^•ﻌ•^ fow things wike h-handwing the pwayew i-input contwows, this wouwd wesuwt in annoying wag, ^•ﻌ•^ s-so you shouwd p-pwobabwy fix it.

expwicit system owdewing

if a specific system must awways w-wun befowe ow aftew s-some othew systems, you can add owdewing constwaints:

change detection

wewevant officiaw exampwes: component_change_detection.

bevy awwows you to easiwy detect w-when data is changed. OwO y-you can use t-this to pewfowm actions in wesponse to changes.

one of the main use cases is optimization – a-avoiding u-unnecessawy w-wowk by onwy doing it if the wewevant data h-has changed. OwO anothew u-use case i-is twiggewing speciaw actions to occuw on changes, OwO w-wike configuwing s-something ow s-sending the data somewhewe.

components

fiwtewing

you can make a quewy that onwy yiewds entities if specific components on them have been modified.

use quewy fiwtews:

  • Added<T>: detect nyew component instances
    • if the component was added to an e-existing entity
    • if a nyew entity with the component w-was spawned
  • Changed<T>: detect component instances that h-have been changed
    • twiggews when the component is accessed m-mutabwy
    • awso twiggews if the component is n-nyewwy-added (as p-pew Added)

(if you want to weact to wemovaws, (ꈍᴗꈍ) s-see the page on wemovaw detection. >_< it wowks diffewentwy and is much twickiew to use.)

fn debug_stats_change(
    q-quewy: quewy<
        // c-components
        (&heawth, 😳 &pwayewxp),
        // f-fiwtews
        (without<enemy>, XD o-ow<(changed<heawth>, :3 c-changed<pwayewxp>)>), 😳😳😳 
    >, -.-
) {
    f-fow (heawth, ( ͡o ω ͡o ) xp) in quewy.itew() {
        epwintwn!(
            "hp: {}+{}, rawr x3 xp: {}", nyaa~~
            heawth.hp, /(^•ω•^) h-heawth.extwa, rawr xp.0

    }

/// detect nyew e-enemies and pwint theiw heawth
f-fn debug_new_hostiwes(
    quewy: quewy<(entity, OwO &heawth), (U ﹏ U) added<enemy>>,

note that change detection cannot c-cuwwentwy be used t-to detect states changes (via the State wesouwce) (bug).

nani gets detected?

Changed detection is twiggewed by DerefMut. (ꈍᴗꈍ) simpwy accessing components via a-a mutabwe quewy, without actuawwy pewfowming a &mut access, XD wiww not twiggew it.

this makes change detection quite a-accuwate. OwO you can w-wewy on it to o-optimize youw game's pewfowmance, ^•ﻌ•^ ow to othewwise t-twiggew t-things to happen.

awso nyote that when you mutate a c-component, OwO bevy d-does nyot twack i-if the nyew vawue is actuawwy diffewent fwom t-the owd vawue. OwO it w-wiww awways twiggew t-the change detection. ^•ﻌ•^ if you want to a-avoid that, OwO simpwy c-check it youwsewf:

fn update_pwayew_xp(
    mut quewy: q-quewy<&mut pwayewxp>, UwU
) {
    f-fow mut xp in quewy.itew_mut() {
        w-wet nyew_xp = m-maybe_wvw_up(&xp);

        // a-avoid twiggewing c-change detection i-if the v-vawue is the same
        if nyew_xp != *xp {
            *xp = nyew_xp;
        }
    }
}

change detection wowks on a pew-system gwanuwawity, >_< and is wewiabwe. OwO a system wiww nyot detect c-changes that i-it made itsewf, 🥺 o-onwy those done by othew systems, OwO and onwy if i-it has nyot seen t-them befowe (the c-changes happened since the wast time it wan). ^•ﻌ•^ i-if youw system o-onwy wuns sometimes (such as with states ow wun cwitewia), you do not have to wowwy about missing changes.

possibwe pitfawws

bewawe of fwame deway / 1-fwame-wag. ^•ﻌ•^ this can occuw i-if bevy wuns t-the detecting system befowe the changing system. OwO t-the detecting s-system wiww see t-the change the nyext time it wuns, ^•ﻌ•^ typicawwy o-on the nyext fwame u-update.

if you nyeed to ensuwe that changes a-awe handwed immediatewy / d-duwing t-the same fwame, XD you can use expwicit system owdewing.

howevew, (ꈍᴗꈍ) when detecting component a-additions with Added<T> (which awe typicawwy done using Commands), XD this is nyot enough; you nyeed stages.

states

wewevant officiaw exampwes: state.

considew using the iyes_loopless cwate, XD which pwovides an awtewnative impwementation t-that does n-nyot suffew fwom t-the usabiwity issues of the one in bevy.

states awwow you to stwuctuwe the w-wuntime "fwow" o-of youw app.

this is how you can impwement things w-wike:

  • a menu scween ow a woading scween
  • pausing / unpausing the game
  • diffewent game modes
  • …

in evewy state, >_< you can have diffewent systems wunning. XD you can awso add one-shot setup and cweanup s-systems to w-wun when entewing o-ow exiting a state.

to use states, (ꈍᴗꈍ) define an enum type a-and add system sets to youw app buiwdew:

    p-paused, mya

                .with_system(handwe_ui_buttons)

            s-systemset::on_entew(appstate::mainmenu)
                .with_system(setup_menu)
        )

        .add_system_set(
            systemset::on_exit(appstate::mainmenu)
                .with_system(cwose_menu)
        )

}

it is ok to have muwtipwe system s-sets fow the same s-state.

this is usefuw when you want to pwace wabews and use expwicit system owdewing.

this can awso be usefuw with pwugins. >_< each pwugin can add its own set of systems to the same s-state.

states awe impwemented using wun cwitewia undew the hood. these speciaw system set constwuctows a-awe weawwy j-just hewpews to a-automaticawwy add the state management wun cwitewia.

contwowwing states

to change to anothew state:

aftew the systems of the cuwwent s-state compwete, OwO b-bevy wiww twansition t-to the nyext state you set.

you can do awbitwawiwy many state t-twansitions in a-a singwe fwame update. OwO b-bevy wiww handwe aww of them and exekawaii~ a-aww the wewevant s-systems (befowe m-moving on to the nyext stage).

state stack

instead of compwetewy twansitioning f-fwom one state t-to anothew, OwO you c-can awso ovewway states, >_< fowming a stack.

this is how you can impwement things w-wike a "game p-paused" scween, OwO o-ow an ovewway menu, OwO with the game wowwd s-stiww visibwe / w-wunning in the b-backgwound.

you can have some systems that awe s-stiww wunning e-even when the state i-is "inactive" (that is, ^•ﻌ•^ in the backgwound, OwO with othew s-states wunning o-on top). 🥺 you can awso add one-shot systems to w-wun when "pausing" o-ow "wesuming" t-the state.

in youw app buiwdew:

            s-systemset::on_update(appstate::ingame)
                .with_system(pwayew_movement)

            systemset::on_wesume(appstate::ingame)

                .with_system(setup_pwayew)
                .with_system(setup_map)

to manage states wike this, >_< use push/pop:

    a-app_state.push(appstate::paused).unwwap();
    // t-to go back i-into the game
    a-app_state.pop().unwwap();

(using .set as shown befowe wepwaces the active s-state at the t-top of the stack)

known pitfawws and wimitations

combining with othew wun cwitewia

because states awe impwemented using wun cwitewia, they cannot be combined with othew u-uses of wun cwitewia, ^•ﻌ•^ s-such as fixed timestep.

if you twy to add anothew wun cwitewia t-to youw system s-set, OwO it wouwd w-wepwace bevy's state-management wun cwitewia! OwO t-this wouwd m-make the system s-set nyo wongew constwained to wun as pawt o-of a state!

considew using iyes_loopless, XD which does nyot have such wimitations.

muwtipwe stages

bevy states cannot wowk acwoss muwtipwe stages. XD wowkawounds awe avaiwabwe, (ꈍᴗꈍ) but they awe bwoken a-and buggy.

this is a huge wimitation in pwactice, OwO a-as it gweatwy w-wimits how you c-can use commands. (ꈍᴗꈍ) nyot being abwe to use commands i-is a big deaw, as you cannot do things wike spawn e-entities and opewate o-on them duwing t-the same fwame, (ꈍᴗꈍ) among othew impowtant u-use cases.

considew using iyes_loopless, XD which does nyot have such wimitations.

with input

if you want to use Input<T> to twiggew state twansitions using a button/key pwess, ^•ﻌ•^ you nyeed to c-cweaw the input m-manuawwy by cawwing .reset:

    mut keys: wesmut<input<keycode>>, òωó
    m-mut app_state: w-wesmut<state<appstate>>, o.O
) {
    i-if keys.just_pwessed(keycode::escape) {
        a-app_state.set(appstate::mainmenu).unwwap();
        k-keys.weset(keycode::escape);
    }

(note that this wequiwes ResMut)

not doing this can cause issues.

iyes_loopless does nyot have this issue.

events

when weceiving events in systems that don't wun aww the t-time, (ꈍᴗꈍ) such as duwing a pause state, OwO you wiww m-miss any events t-that awe sent duwing t-the fwames when the weceiving systems awe nyot w-wunning!

to mitigate this, (ꈍᴗꈍ) you couwd impwement a-a custom cweanup stwategy, (ꈍᴗꈍ) to manuawwy manage the wifetime o-of the wewevant event types.

wun cwitewia

considew using the iyes_loopless cwate, XD which pwovides an awtewnative impwementation t-that does n-nyot suffew fwom t-the usabiwity issues of the one in bevy.

wun cwitewia awe a mechanism fow c-contwowwing if bevy s-shouwd wun specific systems, (ꈍᴗꈍ) at wuntime. this is how you can m-make functionawity that onwy wuns undew cewtain conditions.

wun cwitewia can be appwied to individuaw systems, rawr x3 system sets, XD and stages.

wun cwitewia awe bevy systems that w-wetuwn a vawue o-of type enum ShouldRun. >< they can accept any system pawametews, >< wike a nyowmaw system.

this exampwe shows how wun cwitewia m-might be used t-to impwement diffewent muwtipwayew modes:

#[dewive(debug, rawr x3 pawtiaweq, eq)]
#[dewive(wesouwce)]
e-enum muwtipwayewkind {
    c-cwient, mya
    host, nyaa~~
    w-wocaw, (⑅˘꒳˘)
}

f-fn wun_if_connected(
    m-mode: w-wes<muwtipwayewkind>, rawr x3
    s-session: w-wes<mynetwowksession>, (✿oωo)
) -> shouwdwun
{
    if *mode == muwtipwayewkind::cwient && session.is_connected() {
        shouwdwun::yes
    } e-ewse {
        shouwdwun::no
    }
}

fn wun_if_host(

known pitfawws

combining muwtipwe wun cwitewia

it is nyot possibwe to make a system t-that is conditionaw o-on muwtipwe w-wun cwitewia. >_< bevy has a .pipe method that awwows you to "chain" w-wun cwitewia, which couwd wet you modify the output o-of a wun cwitewia, OwO b-but this i-is vewy wimiting in pwactice.

considew using iyes_loopless. XD it awwows you to use any nyumbew of wun conditions t-to contwow youw s-systems, OwO and does n-nyot pwevent you fwom using states ow fixed timestep.

events

when weceiving events in systems that don't wun evewy f-fwame, you wiww miss any events that awe s-sent duwing the f-fwames when the w-weceiving systems awe nyot wunning!

to mitigate this, (ꈍᴗꈍ) you couwd impwement a-a custom cweanup stwategy, (ꈍᴗꈍ) to manuawwy manage the wifetime o-of the wewevant event types.

wabews

you nyeed wabews to nyame vawious t-things in youw app, XD such as systems (fow owdew contwow), rawr x3 wun cwitewia, rawr x3 stages, XD and ambiguity sets.

the most common use fow wabews is f-fow system owdewing and adding stages.

bevy uses some cwevew wust type system m-magic, OwO to a-awwow you to use s-stwings as weww as youw own custom types f-fow wabews, ^•ﻌ•^ and e-even mix them!

using stwings fow wabews is quick a-and easy fow pwototyping. OwO h-howevew, 🥺 t-they awe easy to mistype and awe unstwuctuwed. OwO t-the compiwew c-cannot vawidate t-them fow you, >_< to catch mistakes.

you can awso use custom types (usuawwy enums) to define youw wabews. >_< this awwows the compiwew to check them, OwO a-and hewps you s-stay owganized in w-wawgew pwojects.

you nyeed to dewive the appwopwiate t-twait, OwO depending o-on nyani they w-wiww be used fow: StageLabel, rawr x3 SystemLabel, rawr x3 RunCriteriaLabel, XD ow AmbiguitySetLabel.

any wust type is suitabwe, OwO as wong a-as it has the f-fowwowing standawd w-wust twaits: Clone (and the impwied Send + Sync + 'static).

stages

aww systems to be wun by bevy awe contained i-in stages. (ꈍᴗꈍ) evewy fwame update, OwO bevy exekawaii~s each s-stage, 🥺 in owdew. òωó w-within each s-stage, o.O bevy's scheduwing awgowithm can wun many s-systems in pawawwew, OwO u-using muwtipwe c-cpu cowes fow good pewfowmance.

the boundawies between stages awe e-effectivewy hawd s-synchwonization p-points. they ensuwe that aww systems of the p-pwevious stage h-have compweted b-befowe any systems of the nyext stage begin, OwO a-and that thewe i-is a moment in time w-when nyo systems awe in-pwogwess.

  • in the main app (CoreStage, >_< wun evewy fwame update): First, rawr x3 PreUpdate, rawr x3 Update, rawr x3 PostUpdate, rawr x3 Last
  • in the wendew sub-app (RenderStage): Extract, rawr x3 Prepare, rawr x3 Queue, rawr x3 PhaseSort, rawr x3 Render, rawr x3 Cleanup

by defauwt, ^•ﻌ•^ when you add youw systems, OwO t-they awe added t-to CoreStage::Update. >_< stawtup systems awe added to StartupStage::Startup.

if you want to add youw own systems t-to any of bevy's i-intewnaw stages, OwO y-you need to bewawe of potentiaw unexpected i-intewactions w-with bevy's own i-intewnaw systems. OwO wemembew: bevy's intewnaws a-awe impwemented u-using owdinawy s-systems and ecs, >_< just wike youw own stuff!

if you nyeed to manage when youw s-systems wun, OwO wewative t-to one anothew, 🥺 i-it is genewawwy pwefewabwe to avoid u-using stages, and t-to use expwicit system owdewing instead. (ꈍᴗꈍ) stages wimit pawawwew execution a-and the pewfowmance of youw game.

howevew, OwO stages can make it easiew t-to owganize things, 🥺 w-when you weawwy w-want to be suwe that aww pwevious systems h-have compweted. OwO s-stages awe awso t-the onwy way to appwy commands.

system piping

wewevant officiaw exampwes: system_piping.

you can compose a singwe bevy system fwom muwtipwe wust functions.

pewfowmance wawning

excwusive systems awe systems that bevy wiww not wun in pawawwew with any othew system. >_< they can have fuww unwestwicted access to the whowe ecs World, XD by taking a &mut World pawametew.

inside of an excwusive system, OwO you h-have fuww contwow o-ovew aww data s-stowed in the ecs. (ꈍᴗꈍ) you can do nyanievew y-you want.

note that excwusive systems can wimit p-pewfowmance, ^•ﻌ•^ a-as they pwevent muwti-thweading (nothing ewse wuns at the same time).

some exampwe situations whewe excwusive s-systems awe u-usefuw:

  • diwectwy spawn/despawn entities, XD ow cweate/wemove wesouwces, immediatewy with nyo deway (unwike w-when using Commands fwom a weguwaw system)
  • wun awbitwawy systems with youw own s-scheduwing awgowithm
  • …

    // w-we c-can do anything w-with any data in t-the bevy ecs hewe! 🥺
}

you nyeed to add excwusive systems t-to the app, XD just wike weguwaw systems, but you must caww .exclusive_system() on them.

they cannot be owdewed in-between w-weguwaw pawawwew s-systems. OwO excwusive s-systems awways wun at one of the fowwowing p-pwaces:

  • .at_start(): at the beginning of a stage
  • .at_end(): at the end of a stage, aftew commands fwom weguwaw systems have been appwied
  • .before_commands(): aftew aww the weguwaw systems in a-a stage, but befowe commands awe appwied

(if you don't specify anything, (ꈍᴗꈍ) the d-defauwt is assumed .at_start())

    app::new()
        .add_pwugins(defauwtpwugins)

        // this w-wiww wun at the s-stawt of cowestage::update (the d-defauwt stage)
        .add_system(do_cwazy_things)

        // t-this wiww wun at t-the end of cowestage::postupdate
        .add_system_to_stage(
            c-cowestage::postupdate, o.O
            some_mowe_things
                .at_end()
        )

tabwe stowage

tabwe stowage is optimized fow fast quewy itewation. XD if the way you usuawwy use a specific component t-type is t-to itewate ovew i-its data acwoss many entities, (ꈍᴗꈍ) this wiww offew t-the best pewfowmance.

you can see why tabwe stowage was c-chosen as bevy's d-defauwt. OwO most c-component types awe wawewy added/wemoved in p-pwactice. spawse-set stowage is optimized fow f-fast adding/wemoving o-of a component t-to existing entities, OwO at the cost of s-swowew quewying. 🥺 i-it can be mowe e-efficient fow components that you wouwd wike t-to add/wemove v-vewy fwequentwy.

tabwe fwagmentation

fuwthewmowe, OwO the actuaw memowy wayout o-of the "tabwes" d-depends on t-the set of aww tabwe components that each of y-youw entities has.

ecs quewies pewfowm best when many o-of the entities t-they match have t-the same ovewaww set of components.

ovewaww advice

manuaw event cweawing

cwick hewe to downwoad a fuww exampwe f-fiwe with the c-code fwom this p-page.

the event queue nyeeds to be cweawed pewiodicawwy, so that it does not gwow indefinitewy a-and waste unbounded m-memowy.

bevy's defauwt cweanup stwategy is t-to cweaw events e-evewy fwame, OwO but w-with doubwe buffewing, OwO so that events fwom the p-pwevious fwame u-update stay avaiwabwe. 🥺 t-this means that you can handwe the events o-onwy untiw the e-end of the nyext f-fwame aftew the one when they awe sent.

this defauwt wowks weww fow systems t-that wun evewy f-fwame and check f-fow events evewy time, (ꈍᴗꈍ) which is the typicaw u-usage pattewn.

howevew, OwO if you have systems that d-do nyot wead events e-evewy fwame, 🥺 t-they might miss some events. ^•ﻌ•^ some common scenawios w-whewe this o-occuws awe:

  • systems with an eawwy-wetuwn, OwO that d-don't wead events e-evewy time they w-wun
  • when using fixed timestep
  • systems that onwy wun in specific states, such as if youw game has a pause s-state
  • when using custom wun cwitewia to contwow youw systems

to be abwe to wewiabwy manage events i-in such ciwcumstances, OwO y-you might w-want to have manuaw contwow ovew how wong t-the events awe h-hewd in memowy.

you can wepwace bevy's defauwt cweanup s-stwategy with y-youw own.

to do this, (ꈍᴗꈍ) simpwy add youw event t-type (wwapped as Events<T>) to the app buiwdew using .init_resource, XD instead of .add_event.

(.add_event is actuawwy just a convenience method t-that initiawizes t-the wesouwce and adds bevy's buiwt-in system (genewic ovew youw event type) fow the defauwt c-cweanup stwategy)

you must then cweaw the events at y-youw discwetion. OwO i-if you don't do t-this often enough, (ꈍᴗꈍ) youw events might piwe up a-and waste memowy.

exampwe

/// custom cweanup stwategy fow e-events

    // fow deciding when to cweaw the events

    // cweaw aww e-events wike this:
    events.cweaw();

    // (this is nyani bevy's d-defauwt stwategy does)

    // o-ow dwain t-them, (ˆ ﻌ ˆ)♡ if you want t-to itewate, (˘ω˘)
    // t-to access the vawues:

note: this chaptew of the book is an eawwy wowk in pwogwess! many winks awe stiww bwoken!

wendew awchitectuwe ovewview

note: this chaptew of the book is an eawwy wowk in pwogwess! many winks awe stiww bwoken!

the cuwwent bevy wendew awchitectuwe p-pwemiewed in b-bevy 0.6. ^•ﻌ•^ the news bwog post is anothew pwace you can weawn about i-it. (ꈍᴗꈍ) :)
